    <a title="Alicia Taylor" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13461649-alicia-taylor"><img alt="Alicia Taylor" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1349651437p2/13461649.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/779607043?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alicia Taylor" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alicia Taylor" href="/user/show/13461649-alicia-taylor">Alicia Taylor</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13461649-alicia-taylor?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer779607043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2128443853747996882">WOW. I'm not sure what to say. I did not see half of them twists and turns coming. I've been completely blown away by this series. I never expected it to be so good but it is, by far, better than I ever imagined.<br/><br/>The emotions I got from reading Elite then Elect is outstanding. I was so excited but held in suspense all the way through.<br/><br/>So the love triangle in this series reminds me of the love triangle in Twilight series. Wait before you misunderstand me there. These books are NOT similar to the Tw</span>
  <span id="freeText2128443853747996882" style="display:none">WOW. I'm not sure what to say. I did not see half of them twists and turns coming. I've been completely blown away by this series. I never expected it to be so good but it is, by far, better than I ever imagined.<br /><br />The emotions I got from reading Elite then Elect is outstanding. I was so excited but held in suspense all the way through.<br /><br />So the love triangle in this series reminds me of the love triangle in Twilight series. Wait before you misunderstand me there. These books are NOT similar to the Twilight saga at all. Nothing alike. Both AMAZING for their own reasons but so far apart. What I mean is the love Bella felt for Jacob was never enough to out shine her love for Edward. My feelings for the characters were exactly like Bella's was and just as strong.<br /><br />In the Eagle Elite series it's the same for me. There is not a chance that my feelings and love for Chase can out shine my love for Nixon. Chase may own my heart but Nixon holds my soul. That type of love can never be beaten. I still am and always will be team Nixon!<br /><br />I wasn't sure where Rachel was going to take Elect after the way Elite ended. I have to say, she couldn't have made this book any better, any more amazing or any different. It's in a league of it's own!<br /><br />5 stars baby!! #TeamNixon</span>
  <a data-text-id="2128443853747996882" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('G0Q4jWl/gmnrCDbnoTYuHPwKTtBt8PbWE72KrifNc7xSN8N45gSpwXPBOEiIFA3D+6lWoHXcUfjUO/XH0stf7A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xT9I41J5q36iUQAQ28gn8X1B3xdUOaS+2vdv+rr7yd6MTLMW3QKA1jqYDr/y6gQueuLHZ0wVA5AdcRCTT/3ljg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
